                                          • 3. Do you have any suggestions for improvements to the Introduction to Understanding WCAG 2.0 section?
                                          • 4. Do you have any suggestions for improvements to the Understanding Techniques for WCAG Success Criteria section?

                                          • 6. Please provide any suggestions you have for changes to make the techniques document more useful or easier to use.
                                          • 7. Do you have any suggestions for improvements to these sections (of How To Meet)?
                                          • 8. When customizing the How to Meet WCAG 2.0 resource to show only a specific technology, such as CSS, general techniques are also included. Do you like this? Please provide any comments or thoughts on this behavior you would like to share.
                                          • 10. Please provide any comments on the visual design or informational structure that you feel particularly help or hinder use of the How to Meet WCAG 2.0 resource
                                          • 11. Please provide any suggestions you have for changes to make the How to Meet WCAG 2.0 document more useful or easier to use.
                                          • 12. Are there any other ideas or suggestions that you have that would make implementing support for the WCAG 2.0 success criteria easier for you?

                                        • 18 March: Web Content Accessibility Guidelines Working Group Teleconference
                                          • Joint meeting with Eval Task Force
                                          • Review teams: Do we recommend that website accessibility evaluations are more effective with a team of 2-3 evaluators, as opposed to 1 only?
                                          • Techniques: Can we be more encouraging about the use of techniques (for evaluation!), yet be clear that the SCs are the checking targets?
                                          • Support for evaluators: Throughout the work we've noted that WCAG 2 does not provide adequate support for evaluators and that we will not be able to cover these needs in WCAG-EM -- reporting back to WCAG...
                                          • Scoring: There are many reasons for and against, and different (and strong) opinions within WCAG WG -- how should we move forward on this?
